  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer5202291429718056597">Now an active member of the resistance, Lena has transformed. The nascent rebellion that was underway in <i>Pandemonium</i> has ignited into an all-out revolution in <i>Requiem</i>, and Lena is at the center of the fight. After rescuing Julian from a death sentence, Lena and her friends fled to the Wilds. But the Wilds are no longer a safe haven. Pockets of rebellion have opened through</span>
  <span id="freeText5202291429718056597" style="display:none">Now an active member of the resistance, Lena has transformed. The nascent rebellion that was underway in <i>Pandemonium</i> has ignited into an all-out revolution in <i>Requiem</i>, and Lena is at the center of the fight. After rescuing Julian from a death sentence, Lena and her friends fled to the Wilds. But the Wilds are no longer a safe haven. Pockets of rebellion have opened throughout the country, and the government cannot deny the existence of Invalids. Regulators infiltrate the borderlands to stamp out the rebels.<br /><br />As Lena navigates the increasingly dangerous terrain of the Wilds, her best friend, Hana, lives a safe, loveless life in Portland as the fiancée of the young mayor.<i>Requiem</i> is told from the perspectives of both Lena and her friend Hana. They live side by side in a world that divides them until, at last, their stories converge.</span>

<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/15857058-tania"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1597352897i/15857058._UY100_CR16,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>

<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/15857058-tania">Tania</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Please not a 4th book... <br/>The whole idea was interesting but the development of the story was very poor. I don't think adding a book would do any bette<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Please not a 4th book... <br />The whole idea was interesting but the development of the story was very poor. I don't think adding a book would do any better. <br />Although the message is very clear, the author can´t explain how the society he depict reach that level of depreciation of feelings. Also, he can't fully explain how a society turn so indifferent. <br />I do understand why the author decided to put Lena in the position of not being able of choosing, we as human being act like that these days. But that is not excuse for not making any choice at all... it left a very bad taste in my mouth that she can´t take a decision . <br />Another thing that is completely out of logic is that Lauren uses a metaphor of the book of shhh to explain what Alex did. (The story of Solomon) I mean, Lauren decides to use a story of the Delirya free era for explaining what -full of love Alex - is doing for Lena? <br />I did not quite understand the sacrifice that Joseph had to do for Magdalene... that another story i didn't comprehend... again the author uses this story for explaining what Anabel did for Lena... that sounds contradictory to me. <br /><a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">This is my favorite book of the trilogy!<br/>And if you didn't like the ending, then you didn't understand what the book is about. We don't need to know wh<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">This is my favorite book of the trilogy!<br />And if you didn't like the ending, then you didn't understand what the book is about. We don't need to know what's going to happen next, that's life. The important thing here is to let down our walls as individuals, knowing that maybe sometimes we might fall, but also that there's a chance that we can fly. To take a leap of faith instead of hiding behind our fears. Fear, will only make us prisoners, but there's a promise of freedom when we believe.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/552570953" />
    <a title="Kenzie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6551250-kenzie"><img alt="Kenzie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1599015101p2/6551250.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/552570953?book_show_action=true">Mar 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kenzie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kenzie" href="/user/show/6551250-kenzie">Kenzie</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer552570953" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10582798917211711856"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292674ra/682217.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292674ra/682218.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>That was awful. Completely awful. Holy hell. What happened?<br/><br/><b>Summary of Requiem: Lena leads Julian on to make Alex jealous. That's it. That's the whole book.</b><br/><br/>Lena... what happened to you? You were bland in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11614718.Delirium__Delirium___1_' title='Delirium (Delirium, #1) by Lauren Oliver' rel='nofollow noopener'>Delirium</a>, had this AMAZING character growth in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9593911.Pandemonium__Delirium___2_' title='Pandemonium (Delirium, #2) by Lauren Oliver' rel='nofollow noopener'>Pandemonium</a>, and here? You were petty and whiny and annoying. Criminy. She asked to leave behind a <i>burned, injured, defenseless</i> girl who had just <i>lost her home and family</i> all because she was jealous that Alex <i>talked</i> to her. Way to be a shitty person,</span>
  <span id="freeText10582798917211711856" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292674ra/682217.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292674ra/682218.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That was awful. Completely awful. Holy hell. What happened?<br><br><b>Summary of Requiem: Lena leads Julian on to make Alex jealous. That's it. That's the whole book.</b><br><br>Lena... what happened to you? You were bland in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11614718.Delirium__Delirium___1_" title="Delirium (Delirium, #1) by Lauren Oliver" rel="nofollow noopener">Delirium</a>, had this AMAZING character growth in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9593911.Pandemonium__Delirium___2_" title="Pandemonium (Delirium, #2) by Lauren Oliver" rel="nofollow noopener">Pandemonium</a>, and here? You were petty and whiny and annoying. Criminy. She asked to leave behind a <i>burned, injured, defenseless</i> girl who had just <i>lost her home and family</i> all because she was jealous that Alex <i>talked</i> to her. Way to be a shitty person, Lena!<br><br>The Lena/Hana back and forth POV chapters were okay. Hana's story was better than Lena's story. At least Hana had some character development, unlike anyone else in the book. I didn't even like Lena anymore. Her character growth from the second book was basically stomped out. Instead of character development, she had <i>recession of character development</i>. Julian was totally forgettable here, his only purpose being to make Alex jealous for Lena and not having any further character development either. Guess it was all used up in Pandemonium. (SUCH GOOD CHARACTER DEVELOPMENT IN PANDEMONIUM!!!! WHAT HAPPENED HERE HOLY BALLS).<br><br>Oh, and there was Alex. Alex, who was a HUGE ASSHOLE THE ENTIRE BOOK. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Oh, he wanted to give Lena up and let her go so he decided to lie and hurt her at every chance he got and be a huge asshole instead. HOW SELF-SACRIFICING!!!! BUT NOPE ALL IS FORGIVEN BECAUSE HE LEFT A NOTE THAT SAID FORGIVE ME AND HE STILL LOVES HER!!!! (TOLD TO LENA BY HIS TWO-SECOND GIRLFRIEND THAT HE PROBABLY GOT JUST TO KEEP LENA AWAY AND HURT HER MORE.) THAT EXCUSES EVERYTHING!!!!!!!!<br><br>And because Alex/Lena are endgame during the last five pages of the book, why not just make sure the book is chock-full of Lena/Julian scenes just for the hell of it??? I guess Julian's purpose of teaching Lena how to let go and move on and love again was totally bullshit. Julian, why the hell were you even introduced as a love interest for Lena in the first place then? Just to make a really shitty, unneeded love triangle? Just to be strung along by Lena the entire time for her to make Alex jealous? Biggest cop-out ever. She had absolutely no respect for Julian's feelings at all. Everything was about ALEX. Here, Lena, have another 'really shitty person' award. My respect I had for you in the second book completely vanished.<br><br>Let me quote the one of the last pages of Pandemonium:<br>"Promise me we'll stay together, okay? You and me." - Julian<br>"I promise." - Lena<br>"Don't believe her." - Alex<br><br>YEP, DON'T BELIEVE HER, JULIAN. Also, the start of huge asshole!Alex. <i>Newsflash: You could've tried to give her up and let her go without being a huge asshole.</i> WOAH!!!!!!! Also, this makes no fucking sense in general. Alex wanted to let her go and give her up or some bullshit, so he goes and basically tells someone else who wants to make her happy to back off???? I guess since it can't be him, even though it was HIS decision, it can't be anyone! LOL.<br><br>And then for the hell of it, to top it all off, let's hurry up end it all with the most anti-climactic, lazy ending ever that leaves everybody feeling bereft and disappointed. Like, open-ended isn't bad if it's done right... yeah, this wasn't. All this felt like was a huge cop-out. We find out NOTHING. Besides making an enormous fucking deal out of the stupid love triangle, this book--the SERIES--was all a huge build-up to this moment... and what? I feel like the end was <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=a8Dshk1XfDc" rel="nofollow noopener">Gene Wilder yelling at me</a>. There is waaaay too much shit that's left unresolved. OH WELL AT LEAST ALEX AND LENA GET BACK TOGETHER, THAT'S OBVIOUSLY ALL THAT MATTERS!!!!!!!!!!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I can't even give this two stars. The prose was as beautiful as always, but not even that can save it. My hope that the series could be good after Pandemonium crashed down and I just. I can't. I really don't think a book has ever disappointed me so much. I probably shouldn't have gone in with such high expectations after the greatness that was Pandemonium, but I did.<br><b>ONE FUCKING STAR</b>.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Also, no, bad rating is not from being butthurt about the love triangle not ending in my favor. I wasn't really invested in this series in the first place to really mind either way. I did prefer Julian, but liked Alex as he was in the FIRST BOOK, AKA, a fine fellow and not a huge asshole. Even if I had wanted them to be endgame, this still would've gotten a bad rating from me. Bad rating is from no character development--RECESSION of character development for Lena, Lena being a shitty person in general, shitty empty ending, Alex being shitty, the book's main focus being the stupidly annoying love triangle, and the nonexistent plot being completely unmemorable. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <span id="freeText14806381252218608573" style="display:none">Warning: There might be MINOR spoilers so yea, be warned :)<br><br><b>AFTER READING:</b><br>When Alex and Lena were doing this...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292674ra/682223.gif" width="400" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I looked like this.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292674ra/682224.gif" width="400" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and then this..<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292674ra/682225.gif" width="300" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I CAN'T FREAKING CONTAIN MY STUPID TANGLED EMOTIONS!!!</b><br>okay I'm calm. I.am.calm.<br><br><b>Julian-Lena-Alex:</b><br>Although Julian somewhat grew on me in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9593913.Requiem__Delirium___3_" title="Requiem (Delirium, #3) by Lauren Oliver" rel="nofollow noopener">Requiem</a>, my heart still belongs to Alex. Frankly, Alex din't do a lot in this book. He is not as active as Julian who, though struggling, managed to adapt well in the Wilds. His natural leadership skills are amazing and he is really determined to prove his worth quickly. I think Lena was <i>waaay</i> more whiny when she first became an invalid than the rich kid Julian and I really admired him for that.<br>He also has the urge of protecting Lena though he is not capable of doing that. MWAHAHAHAHAHAHAHA!!!<br>On to Alex. He has another love interest here. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Name's Coral. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> And was trying to avoid Lena and Julian. He was not in real action here actually, mostly he was described as aloof and snobbish especially to Lena and Julian. He often hangs out with the new girl, knees touching blah blah blah. And then he saves Lena's ass. Again. Though Lena managed to save Alex too <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[from the bear. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>Alex is still Alex. The one who is willing to sacrifice his own happiness for Lena's sake. The sweet sweet guy that we all love.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292674ra/682226.gif" width="300" height="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Annabel:</b><br>She and Lena made up :)<br><br><b>Raven, Tack, Hunter, Bram, Lu, Coral:</b><br>They're Lena's constant companions here, although not all of them made through and there is some kind of <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[betrayal <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> that shocks Lena.<br><br><b>Hana:</b><br>She has a MAJOR role in this. She describes how the cure worked on her. Her feelings, or the lack thereof, and her fear that the cure didn't properly work constantly bugs her. I know I hated Hana not so long ago because of her freaking jealousy, but she kinda made up for it. She has contributed greatly to the Invalid's cause, although she is a cured person herself.<br><br><b>Who did Lena choose?</b><br>I love it that Oliver did not spell it out for us. She left me hanging but in a completely content way. I felt satisfied. I know Lena chose <i>him</i> but she is not rushing it. She loves the other one and she will take things slow, figure out how to proceed from there. How to fix things. At least that's the way I thought it meant.<br><br><b>Lauren Oliver:</b><br>I said it before and I'll say it again. YOU ARE A GENIUS. I don't know how you do it but you made my heart happy. You've told a wonderful story that I am sure I'll never forget it. You made Lena so strong but still realistic. She's not a superhuman, not perfect but she's brave. She loves. She cares <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[even for Coral <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, and she stands up for what she believes. Now that's a remarkable heroine. <br><br><b>BEFORE READING:</b><br>OH GEEZ. THIRD BOOK!!! I hope the world won't end in 2012.<br><br>*enters the much dreaded love triangle* surprise surprise! <i>*thousands of rolling eyes</i><br>ooh Aleeeeeeeeex! Your minimal appearance in Pandemonium is not enough!!<br><b>EDIT:</b><br>Anyway, the third book will be from Lena and Hana's POV.. okay.<br>I hope it'll be told from Alex's POV though :( But I guess this story centers more on the political stuff, not the romance dept so putting Hana's POV, being a cured one, fits right. But I kinda hate her. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[She was the one who sold Lena and Alex to the authorities! Envious bitch! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I like Oliver's writing, I hope this book wouldn't disappoint.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_354569465" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/354569465" />
    <a title="l" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9139963-l"><img alt="l" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1471602481p2/9139963.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/354569465?book_show_action=true">Jun 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="l" class="user" itemprop="url" name="l" href="/user/show/9139963-l">l</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer354569465" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4099653192949676118">~EDIT #3~ ACTUAL REVIEW (<b>SPOILERS AHEAD</b>):<br/><br/>Okay, I know <i>a lot</i> of people have read/liked my 'review' for the ending of Pandemonium and the blurb of requiem, but here's my <b>long-awaited</b> review of Lauren Oliver's Requiem.<br/><br/>I'm going to be very, very honest here. I didn't like it. Compared to the awesomeness that was Delirium, this was honestly disappointing. I hate when authors sway to far from the original plot of the series, which was exactly what Lauren Oliver has done in this latest installment. <br/><br/>The</span>
  <span id="freeText4099653192949676118" style="display:none">~EDIT #3~ ACTUAL REVIEW (<b>SPOILERS AHEAD</b>):<br><br>Okay, I know <i>a lot</i> of people have read/liked my 'review' for the ending of Pandemonium and the blurb of requiem, but here's my <b>long-awaited</b> review of Lauren Oliver's Requiem.<br><br>I'm going to be very, very honest here. I didn't like it. Compared to the awesomeness that was Delirium, this was honestly disappointing. I hate when authors sway to far from the original plot of the series, which was exactly what Lauren Oliver has done in this latest installment. <br><br>The first book was an exciting tale about two people who were in love, and were determined to keep it that way, despite the costs. Alex and Lena's love story was thrilling and interesting, due to the circumstances of their illegal romance and having the characters experience emotions that were entirely new to them. The second book added more depth to the rebellion side to the plot, but still continued with a forbidden love story between Lena and Julian (no matter how much we may have hated Julian, it was still true to the trilogy's origins of forbidden love). <br><br>But this book felt sort of...flat. ESPECIALLY since the ending to the last book was so shocking and exciting, the way Oliver continues the story is disappointing.<br><br>Firstly, you'll have to forgive me for leaving out some detail, I read the book over a year ago and I'm only just getting around to the review. But I remember that I was really pissed that the start of this book didn't pick up right after the last book finished. I wanted to know what Lena's immediate reaction was, I wanted to know what was said after "Don't believe her.", I wanted to know their first conversation. I NEEDED TO NOW THESE THINGS BUT I NEVER GOT THE ANSWERS. <br><br>There was no <i>spark</i> between Alex and Lena. Their love had been so passionate and intense in the first book, and I honestly refuse to believe that the air between them was so tense. Like yeah, Julian was a big bump in the road, but knowing Alex he would have understood. She obviously believed he was dead, and grief doesn't equal 'not able to find love again'.<br><br>Overall, I just wasn't interested in the plot either. I was so focused on wanting Alex to reconcile with Lena that nothing else sparked my interest.<br><br>Also, for a book with such bland emotion and frustrating (not in the good way) plot, the ending was <i>awful.</i> Yes, with some books you can get away with an ending that's very brief and vague, but this series needed more. The plot was just too BIG to end like it did. It was in dire need of an explanatory epilogue.<br><br>Oh well, some books are just duds. Whatever.<br><br><br><br><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><br><br><br><br>~EDIT #2~ BLURB THINGY: "After rescuing Julian from a death sentence, Lena and her friends fled to the Wilds. But the Wilds are no longer a safe haven—pockets of rebellion have opened throughout the country, and the government cannot deny the existence of Invalids. Regulators now infiltrate the borderlands to stamp out the rebels, and as Lena navigates the increasingly dangerous terrain, her best friend, Hana, lives a safe, loveless life in Portland as the fiancée of the young mayor. Requiem is told from both Lena’s and Hana’s points of view. The two girls live side by side in a world that divides them until, at last, their stories converge."<br><br>Ha, I love how the description/blurb says NOTHING about Alex coming back. Probably JUST to torture us that wee bit more ;) But I love this, and I can't wait for Lena to meet up again with Hana.<br><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><br><br><br><br>~EDIT~ <b>THE COVER.</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292673ra/682210.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292673ra/682211.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292673ra/682212.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><br><br>This is what my reaction when I realised Alex was back:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292673ra/682213.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>and then this:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292673ra/682214.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>and This is what I did when I saw that it was the last page of the book:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/392192.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and THIS is what I did when I saw the expected publication date of Requiem:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/510635.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and this.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292674ra/682215.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I hope there's someone else out there who understands that in the whole book of Pandemonium, I was basically just waiting for Alex to burst into the situation saying, "I WILL FIX EVERYTHING!".<br>BUT NO. He came on the very last page of the book. Now miss Lauren Oliver is making me wait an awful 8 MONTHS FOR THE NEXT BOOK.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292674ra/682216.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="4099653192949676118" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer249693381" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13960850708488285754"><b><a href='http://bloodybookaholic.blogspot.com/2014/06/the-delirium-tv-show-is-back-in-action.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Delirium TV SHOW has been picked up again, BY HULU. TO be aired on June 20th, 2014!</a> </b><br/><br/><s>
  <a href='http://bloodybookaholic.blogspot.com/2013/01/from-book-to-tv-delirium-by-lauren.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Holy shit! Delirium, by Lauren Oliver, is to become a TV Show!</a>
</s><br/><br/><a href='http://bloodybookaholic.blogspot.com/2013/02/tvmovie-news-delirium-lauren-oliver-tv.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Delirium, Lauren Oliver, TV Show has it's Lena!! Lena has been cast, guys!</a><br/><br/><a href='http://bloodybookaholic.blogspot.com/2013/02/want-little-taste-of-requiem-3rd-and.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Click here to read 86 juicy pages of Requiem, <s>plus an exclusive short story about ALEX!!!</s>* (DYYING INSIDE!!)</a><br/><br/><a href='http://bloodybookaholic.blogspot.com/2013/03/delirium-tv-show-casting-alex-and-hana.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Delirium TV Show Casting: Alex and Hana have been cast... for better or worse?</a><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292674ra/682219.gif' width='230' height='199' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>...there is another book right?<br/><br/>The DELIRIUM series cannot end this way, so vague a</span>
  <span id="freeText13960850708488285754" style="display:none"><b><a href="http://bloodybookaholic.blogspot.com/2014/06/the-delirium-tv-show-is-back-in-action.html" rel="nofollow noopener">The Delirium TV SHOW has been picked up again, BY HULU. TO be aired on June 20th, 2014!</a> </b><br><br><s>
  <a href="http://bloodybookaholic.blogspot.com/2013/01/from-book-to-tv-delirium-by-lauren.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Holy shit! Delirium, by Lauren Oliver, is to become a TV Show!</a>
</s><br><br><a href="http://bloodybookaholic.blogspot.com/2013/02/tvmovie-news-delirium-lauren-oliver-tv.html" rel="nofollow noopener">The Delirium, Lauren Oliver, TV Show has it's Lena!! Lena has been cast, guys!</a><br><br><a href="http://bloodybookaholic.blogspot.com/2013/02/want-little-taste-of-requiem-3rd-and.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Click here to read 86 juicy pages of Requiem, <s>plus an exclusive short story about ALEX!!!</s>* (DYYING INSIDE!!)</a><br><br><a href="http://bloodybookaholic.blogspot.com/2013/03/delirium-tv-show-casting-alex-and-hana.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Delirium TV Show Casting: Alex and Hana have been cast... for better or worse?</a><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292674ra/682219.gif" width="230" height="199" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>...there is another book right?<br><br>The DELIRIUM series cannot end this way, so vague and unfinished.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292674ra/682220.gif" width="245" height="175" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Disappointed doesn't begin to cover how I feel.<br><br>The beginning was slow, and the ending was rushed, sooo rushed... and unclear, and incomplete, and preachy, and not at all what I was expecting. It felt short, the whole book did.<br><br>So she went back to the wilds and lived crappily ever after? Is that what I am getting?<br><br>Felt like a bridge between books, nothing was really solved, and we were left with more questions than answers. While Pandemonium was a revelation, Requiem was the book that fell short. Guess it was too much to hope Requiem would be just as good. We get NO answers. At the end it's like nothing is resolved, not even the love triangle (that no one believed in the first place anyways).<br><br>I was already suspecting this was going to happen, when I reached the middle of the book (and a little after) and <b>nothing</b> significant had yet happened. We got a confrontation in the romance department (ONE! And not even after they meet face to face for the first time, woah was I pissed!), true, but other than that? Nada!!<br><br>This book was definitely dissapointing. We still get beautiful writing, and it was GREAT to get to see the characters we love again, but it felt like a bridge book. No resolution, no ENDING. Just, all left in the air...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380292674ra/682221.gif" width="250" height="140" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The rest of this review shall be full of spoilers, so read if you must, I have a lot of talking to do about specific parts that pissed.me.off.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[By the end there she is with a child (Grace), reconciles with Alex (barely?) yet hasn't broken up with Julian even though she finally realized she will never love him as much as she loves Alex (DUH!)<br><br>Their reconciliation (Alex and Lena) wasn't even that romantic or sweet. It was business like. Oh yeah I love you, you love me, let's not even make eye contact as we are saying this in THE MIDDLE OF A FUCKING ATTACK.<br><br>Then Lena goes off, stares at Julian's bare chest on her way to a half pummeled wall (guess old habits die hard?) WITH A CHILD to help tear it down some more? WHAT THE HELL IS SHE GOING TO DO? ATTACK THE WALL WITH HER FISTS? SHE AIN'T FUCKING MADE OF STEEL! And the most ridiculous thing of all is the last paragraph where Lauren Oliver tries to tie everything with words of wisdom that quite frankly fell flat.<br><br>After everything we went through Delirium and Pandemonium do you really think a half assed paragraph was going to make me HAPPY? I am furious! The last paragraph could be summarized with the song by Avril Lavigne titled "Keep Holding on". Does this mean we get a sequel? To hold on for a brighter tomorrow in which the ending to one of my favorite series isn't this? I damn hope so.<br><br>And I haven't even started talking about Hana's grand finale.<br><br>She finds out there is a bomb at the house she is to live with her fucking psycho jerk of a husband and she just goes off the backdoor, never looking back. Did the husband explode? WHO KNOWS! Did Hana ever find Lena again? No fucking clue. What is she going to do now? Hell, you got me there!<br><br>And the way she does a complete 180 there at the end on the way she treats Lena and stuff after everything we have read from her POV? Nope, don't believe it. She treats Lena like she barely knows her even though she has been agonizing about her in every other page we read. Dumbfounding!<br><br>Is Hana's husband (the creepy psycho new mayor that quite possibly killed his father) even dead? No one knows! I didn't read about an explosion, how about you?<br><br>Oh and why doesn't Lena break up with Julian? My personal opinion is that Lauren Oliver dug herself a deep hole she doesn't want to get herself out of. Julian only joined the resistance because of Lena, only to find out this girl has been stringing him along this whole time?<br>Fuck, if she series were to continue Julian could become the ultimate super villain! He is smart, hot, from a well respected family, and has a bone to pick with love. Ultimate Super Villain. Couldn't blame the guy.<br><br>And Alex? Don't make me talk about him now, MY Alex died in Delirium. This new ball of hatred is not Alex. He is just not the guy any of us fell in love with, and you know why? BECAUSE HE DOESN'T GET ENOUGH PAGE TIME. If Hana could tell her story by GODS let Alex tell his side! All we get is confused old Lena who doesn't know her ass from her elbows.<br><br>I am sure our Alex never return because he never got a chance. So much time was put into veering us into the wrong conclusion of who was going to win Lena's heart that we didn't have enough reading space to fall in love with Alex all over again, hell we didn't even have time to reconnect!<br><br>Lena and her mother reunite. That was done right, I believe it. Lena is a big ball of feels, she would have forgiven her mother that easily. She never spoke top her about Alex though, in the entire book. You would think that small part of her live (the entire first book right?) would come up in conversation.<br><br>Coral, we hate her, we love her... I kind of liked her at the end. She seemed cool when not looked through Lena's eyes.<br><br>The war was never resolved. They won a battle (I think? They were definitely halfway through when the book ended...) in Portland, but they definitely didn't win any wars! <br><br>OH and after reading Raven's story, to find out she was pregnant (something that was NEVER referred to or addressed in Requiem) and she just DIES? Not even fighting or like the leader she is, she is climbing up some stairs, pokes her head out, and gets shot. Tack comes to console her, and we never read about them two again. Was the shot fatal? Maybe! Was she still pregnant by then? I don't know? Did Tack know? etc etc, nothing was addressed and everything was left up in the air. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a title="Follow Bloody Bookaholic on Bloglovin" href="http://www.bloglovin.com/en/blog/1259979" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img alt="Follow on Bloglovin" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380292674i/682222.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Old updates:<br><br>*Now in order to read the Alex short story you would have to buy a first edition copy of Requiem. Like we weren't doing that anyways!<br><br>Edit 9/20/12<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/544742.gif" width="291" height="233" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Am I the only one who is completely jealous and wants to scream at the top of her lungs to the gods because some people have already read this book and not me? AM I THE ONLY ONE?<br><br>I can't possibly be!<br><br>--<br><br>I know burning books is bad, but if Lena doesn't end up with Alex there will be blood. Julian was a good distraction, and hell he was so cute all around, but Alex pulls at my heart strings. Gosh that ending [Pandemonium] was awesome, the whole book was written perfectly. Lauren Oliver is very very talented. You got a fan in me.<br><br>ADD 6/30/2012:<br><br>HOLY CRAP! There is a cover, there's a cover, there's a cover!!!<br><br>I looove the photo quality, and the color, and the flowers, and EVERYTHING!! I'm just a fan that is full of love for this beautiful cover of one of my favorite series EVER.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_291461289" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/291461289" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4895946-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1359335656p2/4895946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/291461289?book_show_action=true">Mar 09, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/4895946-laura">Laura</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4895946-laura?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4895946-laura?shelf=horrible">horrible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4895946-laura?shelf=not-worth-my-time">not-worth-my-time</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4895946-laura?shelf=hated-it">hated-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4895946-laura?shelf=train-wreck">train-wreck</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer291461289&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer291461289" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6789637598747331902">Due to unfortunate circumstances, I have dropped the rating on this book from 5 stars to a mere 2. <br/><br/>I’m sorry. I just pulled the rug out from under your feet, didn’t I? <br/><br/>Now there are many wonderful, amazing things about this book that I could talk about, however…you probably wouldn’t be reading this if you were in it for the good stuff. You would be reading the book instead. So I’m going to skip all of the fluffy, do-good particles that this book is made of, and delve deeper into the reason for m</span>
  <span id="freeText6789637598747331902" style="display:none">Due to unfortunate circumstances, I have dropped the rating on this book from 5 stars to a mere 2. <br><br>I’m sorry. I just pulled the rug out from under your feet, didn’t I? <br><br>Now there are many wonderful, amazing things about this book that I could talk about, however…you probably wouldn’t be reading this if you were in it for the good stuff. You would be reading the book instead. So I’m going to skip all of the fluffy, do-good particles that this book is made of, and delve deeper into the reason for my rating change. <br><br>I anticipated <i>Requiem</i> ever since the cliffhanger at the end of <i>Pandemonium</i> (which I loved, by the way) and literally counted down the days to its release (I even wrote it on my calendar. And who uses calendars anymore, amirite?) <br><br><i>Pandemonium</i> was a page turner. It had everything that I’d ever wanted in a book – unique writing that seemed almost vivid and scarily real, lots of character development, and the ending just – UHHH. The ending picked you up and slammed you down right as we figure out that Alex is alive. Just before it kicks the door closed: <i>sorry! You have to wait until the next book comes out to see what happened afterwards!</i>. <br><br>And so I waited. Patiently, twiddling my thumbs, watching anime and crying about it, you know – the stuff I do. I re-read <i>Delirium</i> and <i>Pandemonium</i> over again, just to get myself ready for what was sure to be the most AH-MAZ-ING CONCLUSION TO ANY SERIES EVER. <br><br>ANNNNDDDDDD IT STARTS OFF…with nothing. <br><br><i>Nothin’</i>. <br><br>… <br><br>Oh sure, <i>Pandemonium</i> can start off right where Delirium ended, but this book can’t do the same, especially when I sensed an ass-whoopin’ coming? Naw, that’s just cheap. Let us fast forward and not even care/giveashit about Lena’s first encounter with Alex, after everything that had happened between them. <br><br>But okay, yeah…chilled…I chilled down. I ignored that glaringly obvious <i>thing</i> that I didn’t like, and I continued. <br><br><i>A quarter way through</i>: oh boy, can’t wait for some action to happen. Surely Hana’s going to do something awesome and redeem herself, or Lena’s going to kick some ass…<br><br><i>Half way through</i>: Okay, the action can start any time now…uh…please? I already know who Lena’s going to end up with, but just make it work, k? <br><br><i>Three quarters</i>: Umm…something? Anything? Please? It feels like this book hasn’t even started yet. Can I already be this far in? <br><br>And so, the first three quarters of this book was filled with the kind of blah-blah-blah that belongs in soap operas, with a couple raids thrown here and there. Though, as glued as I was to the amazing/flawless writing, I found myself…disappointed. Nothing major occurs, like what you’d expect in the final book. Hana’s point of view was interesting at times, but definitely not what I imagined her to sound like. Sure, she made a few character developments, but overall, Hana was another bland cured that brought almost nothing to the story line, besides a slightly creepy edge. <br><br>At three quarters in, I couldn’t help but think…<br><br><i>”Is this it? It’s almost the end. Where are the explanations? Where are the revelations? It feels…empty, somehow, like a bunch of pages were ripped out. Did I buy a faulty copy? AND NOT WIN AN ARC? (I’m still frustrated about that, to be honest.)</i> <br><br>At that point, I felt kind of ripped off. The scene with Lena and her mother made me want to tear my hair out – we were never given any explanation, any stories or view from “Bee”. What was it like in the Crypts? How had she managed to climb to the top of the ranks? In such an emotion-filled book, there was no feelings between Lena and her mother. It almost pained me to read their confrontations. <i>
  <b>Lifeless</b>
</i>. Like the time I fell asleep on the library floor at my school after an all-nighter at a relay-for-life. (I was practically a zombie, besides being served ice cream at 3:30 a.m. and someone blasting dubstep in a vain attempt for all of us to stay awake) <br><br>But sure, I could ignore that huge punch in the face. But what I couldn’t handle – and what changed my view on this entire book – was the ending. <br><br>That <i>FUCKING</i> ending. <br><br>I’m sorry. I usually don’t swear in reviews, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[(yes I do) <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>but that needed to be said. How many <i>times</i> have you encountered something so <i>mind-numbingly painful</i> that you just had to let a few choice words slip out? <br><br>And let me tell you – there is nothing more frustrating than <i>Requiem</i>, nay, <i>this whole series’</i> ending. <br><br>Remember when we all read <i>Breaking Dawn</i> when we were all in that cray-cray Twilight phase? Remember how it just <b>ended</b>? It didn’t really have any closure. There was no fight – the fight that everyone was preparing for, that everyone was worried about, the fight that I was completely sure was about to happen – and then everyone just talks. They <i>talk it out for fucks sake</i>. And then it ends. Just like that. It’s like the end of <i>Mockingjay</i>, but worse. <br><br>That’s basically what happens in the end of <i>Requiem</i>. The first two books and the first ¾ of the third hype you up towards a fantastic ending that’s sure to blow your mind – or at least resolve the conflict between main characters. <br><br><b>NOPE</b>. <br><br>It ends. You have no idea what happens to ANYONE. It actually stops halfway through the showdown – they had just barely taken the town, and then the pages run out. <br><br>“I’VE BEEN CHEAPED! RIPPED! BAMBOOZLED!” <br><br>But what angers me the most is the Lena/Alex/Julian triangle. It’s never resolved. It just <i>isn’t</i>. Lena and Alex admit their love for each other, even though Lena has been leading Julian on for this entire time and Lena never talks to Julian at the end. They tear down a wall. You never find out what happens to Hana. You don’t know if any other important characters die – what happened to Tack? Or Hunter and Bram? What about Hana’s almost-husband? Does he actually die? What about Coral? What about Lena’s mother? Her aunt? Jenny? Is Lena ever going to tell Julian that her and Alex are getting back together? What happens after they tear down the wall to the Wilds? Will they take the other towns too? <b>There is no closure</b>. <br><br>How hard would it have been to shove in a little scene in the end, resolving Lena/Alex/Julian, and actually telling what happens afterwards? How hard would it have been to ACTUALLY WRITE AN ENDING? <br><br>“I’VE BEEN LEFT HANGING OFF A CLIFF! WHERE’S THE ROPE? A STICK? ANYTHING, PLEASE!” <br><br>Poor Julian. Selfish Lena led him on, and then once Alex admits his love, she’ll just throw him to the side like he’s nothing. But wait – even Lena says she doesn’t know what’s going to happen next. Will she choose Alex, or Julian? <br><br>“ISN’T THIS WHY WE READ THIS BOOK IN THE FIRST PLACE?”<br><br>Here’s what I think happened – Mrs. Oliver was so concerned about <i>teaching the reader a lesson</i> that she forgot to actually have this book make sense. Her lesson - <i>supposed lesson</i> - is that you’re not supposed to know what happens next. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909093i/3177658.jpg" alt=" photo poker-face2_zpscd1bb684.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">”<br><br>Taking this in a lesson view, as in – “you’re not supposed to know what comes next in love - it’s a valid point. Hearty, even. But taking this from a “I-just-stuck-with-this-series-because-I-though-it-was-awesome-and-was-sorely-dissapointed-when-I-realized-that-the-author-didn’t-even-give-us-an-ending” view, it’s a bit of a dick move. The obvious strain to get this message through overshadowed the actual need to take care of her characters and portray them as something other than the means to get to an actual point (which, in my opinion, never actually came to light). <br><br>If you want something deep and semi-emotional, then this ending should suit to your needs. But the more I thought about it, and since I felt cheated, I refused to this of this as anything other than a sham. <br><br>So, as much as I loved the first two books, <i>Requiem</i> was a mistake. A very bad mistake, seeing as the overall rating for this book dropped from a 4.30 before it was released to almost a 3.87 after it came out.<br><br>That just goes to show that (hopefully) others feel the same way. <br><br>AND NO – <br><br><b>THIS IS NO AN EXCUSE TO WRITE MORE BOOKS and/or MAKE A SPIN-OFF. </b><br><br>PlEaSe DoN’t. <br><br>THIS SERIES HAS BEEN FUCKED UP ENOUGH BY THIS, THANK YOU VERY MUCH. <br><br>(Final rating – 2.5. I’m feeling very generous this afternoon. I have been emotionally ruined. Thank you.) <br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="6789637598747331902" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_352025637" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/352025637" />
    <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy"><img alt="Kat Kennedy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537750381p2/3270188.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/352025637?book_show_action=true">Jun 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat Kennedy" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy">Kat Kennedy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=sci-fi-alicious">sci-fi-alicious</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=to-ya-or-not-to-ya">to-ya-or-not-to-ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=just-plain-bad">just-plain-bad</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=oppressive-dystopian-regime">oppressive-dystopian-regime</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=kat-s-book-reviews">kat-s-book-reviews</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer352025637" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14381463947956423469">Requiem. When all good things must come to an end. A horrible, horrible end that didn’t do any justice to the series. But an end nonetheless. Requiem is like sitting down to a well-deserved, hot pie and relishing every bite until you get to the last one and die of poisoning without ever knowing why or how. There was literally a moment when I got to the last few pages, realized there wasn’t any more and freaked out. From enjoyment for insurmountable anger.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380381359ra/738609.gif' alt='laughing, laughing, then STOP!' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I am a solid believer that Lauren Oliver </span>
  <span id="freeText14381463947956423469" style="display:none">Requiem. When all good things must come to an end. A horrible, horrible end that didn’t do any justice to the series. But an end nonetheless. Requiem is like sitting down to a well-deserved, hot pie and relishing every bite until you get to the last one and die of poisoning without ever knowing why or how. There was literally a moment when I got to the last few pages, realized there wasn’t any more and freaked out. From enjoyment for insurmountable anger.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380381359ra/738609.gif" alt="laughing, laughing, then STOP!" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am a solid believer that Lauren Oliver is a capable, talented author. I also think she’s brave. Not all authors risk venturing into unfamiliar territory. Think how common it is for an author to be writing their fourth or fifth book in a series and starting spinoffs in the same world when even that gets old. It’s clear from Delirium that Oliver was trying on something new. Uncomfortable at first, but I’d felt that in Pandemonium, she had hit her stride. Requiem, the last part of Lena’s journey, seems to have been a new challenge all in its own. One that I didn’t feel Oliver managed to surmount.<br><br>The novel is divvied up into Lena’s POV and Hannah’s POV – sometimes done with more success than other times. Overall, it wasn’t a bad series and Requiem wasn’t necessarily a bad book. It simply could never escape from the premise holding so much more promise than the story could deliver. Compared to other series in this genre, it struggled to hold its own candle. I feel bereft and let down after the promise and goodness that was Pandemonium.<br><br>There are concepts and ideas there. A tale Oliver wants to tell about love – its strengths and pitfalls. The good and the bad. You can see the reaching for it in Requiem. Then a point comes when it seems the tale is abandoned in favour of wrapping it up as soon as possible. Some might call it an open ending. To me an open ending leaves you with thoughtful questions, not a whole lot of blank spaces. To me, Requiem doesn’t have an open ending. It just stops, with little rhyme or reason.<br><br>I’m not even going to talk about anything else that happens or the characters or themes or writing or anything. I refuse. Debate or not, an ending is an ending is an ending. Just because something ended doesn’t mean you gave it an actual ending. Need further proof? Allow me to illuminate on th-<br><br><i>This review also appears on my blog, <a href="cuddlebuggery.com/blog/2013/03/01/review-requiem-by-lauren-oliver/" rel="nofollow noopener">Cuddlebuggery Book Blog</a>.</i> </span>
  <a data-text-id="14381463947956423469" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_358991860" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/358991860" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/358991860?book_show_action=true">Jul 01, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it

Show of hands? For those of you who have, how many of you were hoping for a bunch of <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Alex <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> time? Even though I didn't read the short story of Hana (2.5), I'd probably go ahead and tell you to read it, or at the very least look up a wiki or have a friend spoil it for you like I did, so you get the gist of where Hana's mind is at now.<br><br>Hana's story was eh? Lena's story was eh? The way everything collided at the end was eh? Can problems such as these be worked out with so little effort? <br><br>The ending was (I guess) sort of okay, but also annoyingly open. This is all I can mention. How about we make a deal? For everyone who is reading this trilogy, come back and tell me what you thought of that ending. Maybe I'm overreacting and you will all love it.<br><br><b>If you haven't started this trilogy, should you read it?</b> Maybe. Book 1 was exciting. Book 2 was alright. Book 3 was not necessarily boring...it just all comes down to being anti-climactic for me. Maybe you won't feel the same. I have friends who enjoyed the entire trilogy. This isn't the worst dystopia I've read; that's for sure. <br><br>Btw, this is going to be a t.v. show. So if you like reading books before seeing the story play out on film, then you'll be wanting to pick this up anyway. <br><br>Sorry for the lame review. <div id="review_2873792569" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2873792569" />
    <a title="Charlotte May" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14002983-charlotte-may"><img alt="Charlotte May" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596906925p2/14002983.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2873792569?book_show_action=true">Jun 28, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Charlotte May" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Charlotte May" href="/user/show/14002983-charlotte-may">Charlotte May</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781444722970" href="/book/show/16853922-requiem">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14002983-charlotte-may?shelf=dystopia">dystopia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14002983-charlotte-may?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14002983-charlotte-may?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2873792569" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13965060434578603804"><i> "This is the strange way of the world, that people who simply want to love are instead forced to become warriors." </i><br/><br/>3.5 ⭐️<br/><br/>I've had a rocky time with this trilogy. The first book started out as way too romancy for my taste. But the last two books have really gotten down into the nitty gritty of the politics of this world and I found it much more gripping. <br/><br/>Lena and Julian have made it back to her friends from the Wilds, and have joined the resistance. Alex's return in book 2 pissed me off, we neve</span>
  <span id="freeText13965060434578603804" style="display:none"><i> "This is the strange way of the world, that people who simply want to love are instead forced to become warriors." </i><br /><br />3.5 ⭐️<br /><br />I've had a rocky time with this trilogy. The first book started out as way too romancy for my taste. But the last two books have really gotten down into the nitty gritty of the politics of this world and I found it much more gripping. <br /><br />Lena and Julian have made it back to her friends from the Wilds, and have joined the resistance. Alex's return in book 2 pissed me off, we never really learn how he didn't actually die and how he made it back to the group. But I liked the other characters - Raven, Hunter, Bram etc. (even though they are basically background characters, could definitely have had more depth in their stories.)<br /><br />What was better about Requiem is we get 2 POV's instead of just Lena's all the time (cause she can be damn irritating.) We also get a POV from Hana, Lena's old best friend. We get to see what life is like for her as a 'cured' member of society - about to be pushed into a marriage with the new mayor of Portland. I really liked Hana's character - she was strong in the face of adversity, and it's nice that we get a character's perspective from that side instead of just the resistance side.<br /><br />It is an interesting dystopian world that Lauren Oliver has created here, and I will take into account the fact that this is an older YA. YA has improved drastically since this was written so I can't really fault it the same way I'd fault it if it was written in the last few years for example. <br /><br />Overall, I'd say this series is definitely worth checking out. I don't think I'll reread it, but I don't regret picking them up.<br /><br /><i> "We are always being pushed and squeezed down one road or another. We have no choice but to step forward, and then step forward again, and then step forward again; suddenly we find ourselves on a road we haven't chosen at all." </i></span>
  <a data-text-id="13965060434578603804" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <b>After Reading:</b>
</u><br/>I must say, this is probably my least favorite out of the three books.<br/>It's not horrible (Obviously, since I gave it five stars) but it took <i>forever</i> for the pace to pick up, for it to get interesting.<br/><br/>This book is mostly about the Resistance fighting back (HOORAH!!) but they can't just barge in and fight!   <span id="freeText9477119060196926202" style="display:none"><u>
  <b>After Reading:</b>
</u><br />I must say, this is probably my least favorite out of the three books.<br />It's not horrible (Obviously, since I gave it five stars) but it took <i>forever</i> for the pace to pick up, for it to get interesting.<br /><br />This book is mostly about the Resistance fighting back (HOORAH!!) but they can't just barge in and fight! They must plan first! Making most of the novel planing, not fighting.<br />And we all now that planing is that as fun as fighting...<br /><br />Of course it's not <i>all</i> planning!<br />Since, very much like the last book, this book has alternating chapters.<br />Except this time it's alternating between Lena and Hana.<br />While I liked hearing about what's going on in Hana's life, it made the pace of the book <i>slower</i>. Not much is going on in Hana's life (actually, a lot is happening but nothing that seems to entertain me...)<br /><br />Now that I got all of that out of the way, let me talk about what is of most importance...<br /><b>THE ENDING</b><br />We are all aware that <i>this</i> is the last book.<br />And being the last book, it needs to have a good ending.<br />While the ending did leave a few questions unanswered <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The main question unanswered being Alex or Julian?!?!?! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />But I did like how it ended.<br />It brought a sense that <i>things are going to get better</i>.<br />(forgive me for being cliche but...)To me this is the best kind of ending.<br /><br />And while I am sad to see this series go...<br />I will be very unhappy if this series continues, since I know when a book series needs to end (Cassandra Clare doesn't though. Sorry, had to get it out there) and after that ending, I know it is time for me to let this series go.<br /><br />Until the TV show premieres...<br />Hopefully they won't ruin it...<br /><br /><i>P.S. Forgive me if this "review made no sense</i><br /><br /><u>
  <b>Before Reading:</b>
</u><br /><b>AHHHHHHHHHH!<br />WHY DID PANDEMONIUM HAVE TO END IN A CLIFFHANGER?!<br />I HATE CLIFFHANGERS!</b><br />It's number 1 on the list of things I hate<br /><b>AND TO HAVE THIS BOOK COME OUT IN 2013?<br />AFTER THE WORLD ENDS!!<br />THAT'S TORTURE!<br />TORTURE!<br />IT SHOULD BE CONSIDERED ILLEGAL!</b><br />I would feel so much better if I was able to read a sneak peek<br />like 1 chapter<br />maybe 2<br />maybe 3....<br /><br />Anyway...<br />I really really really really really really want this book<br />really<br />and am I the only one sensing a love triangle in this book?<br /><b>DANG IT!<br />I wish those love triangles were never born!!!!!<b><br /><br /><b>EDIT:<br />OH MY HOLY FREXING DONUTS!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!<br />THE COVER!!!!<br />IT'S HERE!!!!!</b><br />*screams of joy*<br /><br /><b>ANOTHER EDIT:<br />WAIT...<br />WHAT?!!!!!<br />Didn't the release date used to be February?!!!!!!<br />Now it's March!!!!<br />MARCH!!!!!!!!!<br />I HAVE TO WAIT A MONTH LONGER!!!!! :'( </b><br /><br /><b>ANOTHER ONE OF MY NUMEROUS EDITS:<br />YAY!!!!<br />THE WORLD DIDN'T END!!!!!<br />NOW I'LL ACTUALLY GET TO READ THIS BOOK!!!!!</b><br />In March...<br />3 months from now...</b></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="9477119060196926202" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
